  <script language="JavaScript" type="text/javascript">
   function killFrames() {
if (top.location != location) {
if (document.referrer) {
var referrerHostname = get_hostname_from_url(document.referrer);
var strLength = referrerHostname.length;
if ((strLength == 11) &amp;&amp; (referrerHostname != "walmart.com")){  // to take care of http://walmart.com url - length of "walmart.com" string is 11.
top.location.replace(document.location.href);
} else if (strLength != 11 &amp;&amp; referrerHostname.substring(referrerHostname.length - 12) != ".walmart.com") {  // length og ".walmart.com" string is 12.
top.location.replace(document.location.href);
}
}
}
if (top.frames.length!=0)
top.location=self.document.location;
};
function get_hostname_from_url(url) {
return url.match(/:\/\/(.[^/?]+)/)[1];
};
killFrames();
  </script>

var g0041s6HasSearchQuery;
function g0041s6SetSearchQuery(hasSearchQuery, search_queryValue) {
var search_query = document.searchbox.search_query;
if (hasSearchQuery) {
g0041s6HasSearchQuery = true;
search_query.value = search_queryValue;
search_query.style.color = "#333333";
}
else {
g0041s6HasSearchQuery = false;
search_query.value = "Search";
search_query.style.color = "#999999";
}
}
g0041s6SetSearchQuery(WALMART.page.search_query, WALMART.page.search_query);
WALMART.page.g0041s6 = {
validate: function () {
if (!g0041s6HasSearchQuery) {
document.searchbox.search_query.value = "";
}
return true;
}
, focus: function () {
if (!g0041s6HasSearchQuery) {
g0041s6SetSearchQuery(true, "");
}
}
, blur: function () {
if (document.searchbox.search_query.value.length == 0) {
g0041s6SetSearchQuery(false);
}
}
, submit: function () {
return WALMART.page.g0041s6.validate() &amp;&amp; document.searchbox.submit();
}
, set: function (value) {
g0041s6SetSearchQuery(value, value);
}
}

     WALMART.jQuery(document).ready(function($) {
/*click function for fly out hide and show*/
$('.searchMainContainer').text($("#selectedFly.buttonLink").text());
$('#searchMain').click(function(){
$('#searchMain').toggleClass('activeFly');
if($("#optionMain").is(":visible")){
$("#optionMain").hide();
}
else{
$("#optionMain").show();
}
});
/*mouse out function to hide flyout*/
$('.allDep').mouseleave(function(){
$("#optionMain").hide();
$('#searchMain').removeClass('activeFly');
});
/*Option selection logic*/
$('.buttonLink').click(function(){
document.getElementById(searchDeptID).value = $(this).attr('value');
document.searchbox.search_constraint.value = $(this).attr('value');
var searchContent=$(this).text();
$('.searchMainContainer').text(searchContent);
$("#optionMain").hide();
$('#searchMain').removeClass('activeFly');
});
var searchlength = $('.searchMainContainer').text().length;
if(searchlength &lt; 3 || true){
document.getElementById(searchDeptID).value = 0;
document.searchbox.search_constraint.value = 0;
$('.searchMainContainer').text('All');
$("#optionMain").hide();
$('#searchMain').removeClass('activeFly');
}
});

        <script type="text/javascript">
         function GlobalErrorMessages(){
this.n = document.getElementById("ItemErrorSwitch");
this.p = this.n.parentNode;
this.m = document.getElementById("errMessages");
this.o = document.getElementById("norMessages");
this.ismessageavailable = false;
this.errorMsgDiv = document.getElementById("errorMsgDiv");
this.normalMsgDiv = document.getElementById("normalMsgDiv");
this.removeErrors = function(){
if(this.ismessageavailable ==false){
if(this.n.parentNode == this.p)
this.p.removeChild(this.n);
if(document.getElementById("SL_ItemMessage"))
{
document.getElementById("SL_ItemMessage").style.display = "none";
}
globalErrorComponent.clearErrors();
}
}
this.showErrors = function(){
if(this.n.parentNode != this.p){
this.p.appendChild(this.n)
this.ismessageavailable = true;
this.n.style.display = "block";
}
this.errorMsgDiv.style.display="";
this.normalMsgDiv.style.display="none";
}
this.showMsgs = function(){
if(this.n.parentNode != this.p){
this.p.appendChild(this.n)
this.ismessageavailable = true;
this.n.style.display = "block";
}
this.errorMsgDiv.style.display="none";
this.normalMsgDiv.style.display="";
}
this.addErrorMessage = function(msg){
this.m.innerHTML += msg +" "
}
this.addNormalMessage = function(msg){
this.o.innerHTML += msg +" "
}
this.clearErroMessages = function(){
this.m.innerHTML = "";
if(document.getElementById("SL_ItemMessage"))
{
document.getElementById("SL_ItemMessage").style.display = "none";
}
this.ismessageavailable = false;
}
}
var globalErrorMessages = new GlobalErrorMessages();
globalErrorMessages.removeErrors();
        </script>

          var zoomBig, zoomRetry = 3;
function checkMagicZoom() {
if (!zoomRetry) return;
if (!zoomBig) {
zoomBig = WALMART.jQuery("#Zoomer-big .MagicZoomBigImageCont")[0];
if (!zoomBig) return;
}
var s = zoomBig.style;
var w = (s &amp;&amp; s.width) ? parseInt(s.width)  : 0;
var h = (s &amp;&amp; s.height) ? parseInt(s.height) : 0;
if (w &lt; 423/2 || h &lt; 397/2) {
MagicZoom.refresh();
zoomRetry--;
}
}

          <script type="text/javascript">
           WALMART.alternatephotos.AltImage = function(url){ // constructor function
return {
count : 0,
mainImageUrl : null,
imageURL : url,
imageObj : new Image(),
setImageURL : function(imageURL){
this.imageObj.src = imageURL;
}
};
};
WALMART.alternatephotos.util = function() {
var mainImageElement;
var prevMainImage;
var prevImageIndex=1;
var currImageIndex = 1;
var NUMBER_OF_THUMBNAILS = 5;
var imageArray = [];
var imageIndex = 0;
return {
imageArray : imageArray,
NUMBER_OF_THUMBNAILS : NUMBER_OF_THUMBNAILS,
setMainImageElement : function(event){
mainImageElement = document.getElementById("mainImage");
},
setAltImages : function(){
// display leftArrow from 1st thumbnail
if (imageIndex===0) {
document.getElementById("leftArrow").style.visibility="hidden";
} else {
document.getElementById("leftArrow").style.visibility="visible";
}
// display rightArrow with last thumbnail
if (NUMBER_OF_THUMBNAILS &gt;=(this.imageArray.length-imageIndex)) {
document.getElementById("rightArrow").style.visibility="hidden";
} else {
document.getElementById("rightArrow").style.visibility="visible";
}
var imgTagName;
var imgIdx=1;
for(i=imageIndex ; i &lt; Math.min(NUMBER_OF_THUMBNAILS+imageIndex, imageArray.length) ; i++) {
imgTagName="Img"+imgIdx;
imgIdx++;
document.getElementById(imgTagName).src = imageArray[i].imageObj.src;
setImgBorders(imgTagName);
}
},
nextImage : function(event){
if(imageIndex &lt; (imageArray.length-1)){
imageIndex++;
}
WALMART.alternatephotos.util.setAltImages();
},
prevImage : function(event){
if(imageIndex &gt; 0){
imageIndex--;
}
WALMART.alternatephotos.util.setAltImages();
},
showMainImage : function(event){
var imgTagNum = event.data;
// translating img tag number to index in the imageArray
var imgIdx = imgTagNum + imageIndex - 1;
prevMainImage = mainImageElement.src;
if (imageArray[imgIdx]) {
mainImageElement.src = imageArray[imgIdx].mainImageURL;
}
},
showPrevMainImage : function(event){
mainImageElement.src = prevMainImage;
},
changeMagicZoom : function(event) {
var imgTagNum = event.data;
var imgIdx = imgTagNum + imageIndex - 1;
var imgThumbId = "Img"+(imgTagNum + imageIndex);
var zoomer = document.getElementById("Zoomer");
if (zoomer) {
zoomer.href = posterImages[imgIdx];
if (typeof MagicZoom != 'undefined' &amp;&amp; typeof (MagicZoom.refresh) == 'function')
MagicZoom.refresh();
}
prevImageIndex = currImageIndex;
currImageIndex = imgTagNum;
},
onImgBorders : function(event){
this.style.borderColor = "#F47B20";
},
offImgBorders : function(event) {
var imgTagNum = event.data;
if (!WALMART.alternatephotos.util.isSameImage(imgTagNum)){
this.style.borderColor = "#D2D2D2";
} else {
var prevImage = document.getElementById("Img"+prevImageIndex);
if (prevImage){
prevImage.style.borderColor="#D2D2D2";
}
}
},
/**
* Tis method will return True if the image hoover over is the same as the one displayed otherwise false.
* @param imgTagNum
* @return boolean true if hero Image same as current hovered image.
*/
isSameImage : function (imgTagNum){
return currImageIndex == imgTagNum;
}
};
}();
WALMART.$(document).bind('ready',this, WALMART.alternatephotos.util.setMainImageElement);

function setImgBorders(imgTagName) {

thumbID.style.borderStyle = "solid";
thumbID.style.borderColor = "#D2D2D2";

          <script type="text/javascript">
           function getRVIdata(commaSeparatedItemList){
var itemList = commaSeparatedItemList.split(',');
WALMART.recentlyvieweditems.contentHost = 'content-cdn.walmart.com';
if (typeof WALMART.recentlyvieweditems.contentHost == 'undefined') {
WALMART.recentlyvieweditems.contentHost = '';
}
WALMART.recentlyvieweditems.counter = itemList.length;
for (var item in itemList) {
WALMART.recentlyvieweditems.AjaxObject_RecentlyViewed.startRequest(itemList[item]);
}
}
(function ($, undefined) {
var rvi = WALMART.recentlyvieweditems
, RVI = rvi.RecentlyViewedItems
;
rvi.display = "";
rvi.contentHost = "content-cdn.walmart.com";
RVI.imageHost = "http://i2.walmartimages.com";
RVI.itemId = "26619817";
rvi.listOfItems = RVI.getLastThreeRecentlyViewedItemList();
rvi.show
= RVI.areRecentlyViewedItemsSetInCookie("true")
? function () {
if (rvi.display == "") {
//start AJAX call:
getRVIdata(RVI.getRVItemsList('true'));
$("#rvi").css("display", rvi.display);
$("#rviClear").click(function () {
RVI.updatePersistentCookie("true", "-10");
$("#rvi_none").css("display", "");
$("#rvi").css("display", "none");
});
}
}
: function() {
if (rvi.display == "") {
$("#rvi_none").css("display", rvi.display);
}
};
$(window).load( function () {
$("#rvi_wrapper").viewed(rvi.show);
}
);
})(WALMART.jQuery);

}

             <script type="text/javascript">
              function submitToWLorGR(context) {
var formObj = WALMART.bot.PageInfo.getItemPageForm("SelectProductForm");
if (window.variants) {
if (masterFiltered() == null || masterFiltered().length &gt; 1 || (masterFiltered().length == 1 &amp;&amp; window.variants.length == 1)) {
var validation = null;
if (context == 0) {
validation = VariantWidgetSelectorManager.getVariantWidgetSelectorObject('C1I26619817')
.validateSelections("wishList",
0);
} else if (context == 2) {
validation = VariantWidgetSelectorManager.getVariantWidgetSelectorObject('C1I26619817')
.validateSelections("reminderList",
0);
} else {
validation = VariantWidgetSelectorManager.getVariantWidgetSelectorObject('C1I26619817')
.validateSelections("giftRegistry",
0);
}
if (!validation.getValid()) {
globalErrorComponent.displayErrMsg(validation.getError());
return;
}
}
formObj["product_id"].value = masterFiltered()[0].itemId;
formObj["qty"].value = WALMART.bot.PageInfo.selectedQty;
}
else {
formObj["qty"].value = 1;
}
if (context == 0) {
formObj.appendChild(buildHiddenInput('add_to_wish_list', true));
} else if (context == 2) {
formObj.appendChild(buildHiddenInput('add_to_reminder_list', true));
} else {
formObj.appendChild(buildHiddenInput('add_to_gift_reg', true));
}
formObj.submit();
}
             </script>

   <script language="javascript">
    var isNotifyMeSignup = false;
var variantWidgetDiv = '#' + 'C1I26619817' + '_VARIANT_SELECT_OPTIONS';
function moveVariantWidget2ItemPage() { WALMART.$(variantWidgetDiv).appendTo(WALMART.$('#VARIANT_SELECTOR')); }
function moveVariantWidget2NotifyMe() { WALMART.$(variantWidgetDiv).appendTo(WALMART.$('#variantWidgetNotifyMeDiv')); }
function initNotifyMeOverlay() {
isNotifyMeSignup = false;
initNotifyMeVaraintWidget();
trackNotifyMeWhenOOS(this,'[Notify Me button Clicked]');
WALMART.$('body').click(function(e){
if(WALMART.$('#emailMeOverlay:visible').length!=0){
var target = WALMART.$(e.target);
if(target.parents('.ui-dialog').length == 0){
WALMART.$('#emailMeOverlay').wmOverlayFramework({}).wmOverlayFramework('close');
}
}
})
}
function closeNotifyMeOverlay() {
WALMART.$('body').unbind('click')
if (isNotifyMeSignup){ // submit/enter button
closeWithouTrack();
trackNotifyMeWhenOOS(this,'[Notify Me sign-up Success]');
}else { // close/cancel button
trackNotifyMeWhenOOS(this,'[Notify Me sign-up Failed]');
}
WALMART.$('#notifyMe').css('visibility','visible');
if (DefaultItem.hasVariants()) {
moveVariantWidget2ItemPage();
}
}
function closeWithouTrack() {
WALMART.bot.PageInfo.hideElement("notifyMe");
WALMART.bot.PageInfo.hideElement("EMAIL_ME_LINK_3");
WALMART.bot.PageInfo.showElement("NOTIFY_ME_MSG");
}
function initNotifyMeVaraintWidget() {
if (DefaultItem.hasVariants()) {
if(WALMART.bot.PageInfo.selectedVariantId) {
var selector = VariantWidgetSelectorManager.getVariantWidgetSelectorObject('C1I26619817');
WALMART.$('#selectedVariantNotifyMeDiv').html(selector.getSelectedValueString());
WALMART.bot.PageInfo.showElement("selectedVariantNotifyMeDiv");
WALMART.bot.PageInfo.hideElement("variantWidgetNotifyMeDiv");
} else {
moveVariantWidget2NotifyMe();
WALMART.bot.PageInfo.hideElement("selectedVariantNotifyMeDiv");
WALMART.bot.PageInfo.showElement("variantWidgetNotifyMeDiv");
}
WALMART.bot.PageInfo.showElement("variantOverlayMsg");
}
}
function checkEnter(evt) {
var code = window.event? evt.keyCode : evt.which;
if(code == 13)
ajaxSignup();
}
function isValidEmail() {
var re = /^[A-Z0-9._-]+@[A-Z0-9.-]+\.[A-Z]{2,3}$/i;
return re.test(WALMART.$('#notifyMeEmail').val()) &amp;&amp; WALMART.$('#notifyMeEmail').val() != 'you@email.com';
}
function ajaxSignup() {
if (isValidEmail()) {
var itemId = WALMART.bot.PageInfo.selectedVariantId ? WALMART.bot.PageInfo.selectedVariantId :'26619817';
var data = {
'email': WALMART.$('#notifyMeEmail').val(),
'itemId': itemId,
'isOnline': 'true',
'originURL': '',
'storeId': ''
};
WALMART.$.post("/catalog/email_collect.do",data);
isNotifyMeSignup = true;
setNotifyMeClicked(itemId);
WALMART.$("#emailMeOverlay").wmOverlayFramework('close');
} else {
WALMART.bot.PageInfo.showElement("invalidEmailMsg");
WALMART.$('.emailMeMsg').hide();
WALMART.$('#notifyMeEmail').css('border','1px solid #cc0000')
}
}
function setNotifyMeClicked(itemId) {
var ck = getCookie('NOTIFYMECLICKED');
var isNullCookie = (ck == null  || typeof ck == 'undefined' || ck == 'undefined');
ck = isNullCookie ? '': ck;
ck += '|' + itemId + '_' + getCustomerId();
setCookie('NOTIFYMECLICKED',ck,'','','','');
}
WALMART.jQuery(function($){
var placeholder = "you@email.com";
$('.notifyMeEmail')
.focus( function(){
$(this).css({'color':'#333','font':'normal 14px verdana'});
if($(this).val() == placeholder){
$(this).val('')
}
})
.blur(function(){
if(!$(this).val()){
$(this).val(placeholder).css({'color':'#ccc','font':'bold 15px verdana'});
}
});
$('.notifyMeEmail').focus();
});
   </script>

   <script type="text/javascript">
    WALMART.$(document).ready(init_rollOverBubble);
function init_rollOverBubble(){
whatIsThisText = 'Select your local Walmart to see information about products in that store while you browse Walmart.com.';
DEFAULT_WIDTH = "190px";
WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER').wmBubble();
MIN_DISPLAY_TIME = 3500;
WALMART.$(document).click(hideRollover);
WALMART.$("#ROLLOVER").bind("mouseover", setEnteredRollover);
if (WALMART.$('#PUT_Store_Location')) {
WALMART.$('#PUT_Store_Location').bind("mouseover", function(event) {
showPreferredStoreRollover(event, 1);
});
}
if (WALMART.$('#storeRollover_1')) {
WALMART.$('#storeRollover_1').bind("mouseover", function(event) {
showPreferredStoreRollover(event, 1);
});
}

showPreferredStoreRollover(event, 3);
});
}

showPreferredStoreRollover(event, 3);
});
}
}
function setEnteredRollover(e) {
clearTimeout(hideTimer);
if (document.getElementById("ROLLOVER_CLOSE").style.display == 'none') {
setHideTimer(MIN_DISPLAY_TIME);
}
}
function getSourceElementId(e) {
e = (e) ? e : ((window.event) ? window.event : "")
var el = null;
try {
el = e.srcElement.id;
} catch(ex) {
el = e.target.id;
}
return el;
}
function showRollover(e, text, width) {
isRolloverShown = true;
setHideTimer(MIN_DISPLAY_TIME);
resetRollover();
WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER_OTHER_TEXT').show();
WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER_CLOSE').show();
WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER_OTHER_TEXT').html(text);
e = (e) ? e : ((window.event) ? window.event : "")
WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER').wmBubble('position',{top:getY(e, 0),left:getX(e)});
WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER').wmBubble('update',WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER').html());
WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER').wmBubble('show');
}
function showOverlayRollover(x, y) {
isRolloverShown = true;
setHideTimer(MIN_DISPLAY_TIME);
resetRollover();
WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER_OTHER_TEXT').show();
WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER_OTHER_TEXT').html(whatIsThisText);
WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER').wmBubble('position',{top:y,left:x});
WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER').wmBubble('update',WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER').html());
WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER').wmBubble('show');
}
function showPickupHourRollover(x, y, businessHours) {
if (businessHours != undefined &amp;&amp; businessHours.length &gt;= 3) {
var businessHourM2FText = generateBusinessHourText(businessHours[2]);
var businessHourSATText = generateBusinessHourText(businessHours[0]);
var businessHourSUNText = generateBusinessHourText(businessHours[1]);
pickupHourInfo = '&lt;div class="BodyM"&gt;Monday &ndash; Friday&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class="BodyMBold"&gt;'
+ businessHourM2FText
+ '&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div style="font-size:5px;"&gt;&nbsp;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class="BodyM"&gt;Saturday&lt;/div&gt;'
+ '&lt;div class="BodyMBold"&gt;' + businessHourSATText + '&lt;/div&gt;'
+ '&lt;div style="font-size:5px;"&gt;&nbsp;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class="BodyM"&gt;Sunday&lt;/div&gt;'
+ '&lt;div class="BodyMBold"&gt;' + businessHourSUNText + '&lt;/div&gt;';
isRolloverShown = true;
setHideTimer(MIN_DISPLAY_TIME);
resetRollover();
WALMART.$("#ROLLOVER_PICKUP_HOUR").show();
WALMART.$("#ROLLOVER_PICKUP_HOUR").html( pickupHourInfo);
WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER').wmBubble('position',{top:(y-114),left:x});
WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER').wmBubble('update',WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER').html());
WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER').wmBubble('show');
} else {
pickupHourInfo = '&lt;div class="BodyM"&gt;Please call for store hours.&lt;/div&gt;';
isRolloverShown = true;
setHideTimer(MIN_DISPLAY_TIME);
resetRollover();
WALMART.$("#ROLLOVER_PICKUP_HOUR").show();
WALMART.$("#ROLLOVER_PICKUP_HOUR").html(pickupHourInfo);
WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER').wmBubble('position',{top:(y-38),left:x});
WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER').wmBubble('update',WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER').html());
WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER').wmBubble('show');
}
}
function generateBusinessHourText(businessHour) {
if (businessHour) {
openTime = businessHour.openTime;
closeTime = businessHour.closeTime;
if ((openTime == '-1:-1 am' || openTime == '00:00 am') &amp;&amp; closeTime == '00:00 am') {
return 'Closed';
} else if (openTime == '00:00 am' &amp;&amp; (closeTime == '11:59 pm' || closeTime == '-1:-1 am')) {
return 'Open 24 hours';
} else {
return openTime + ' &ndash; ' + closeTime;
}
}
}

* This method added for VIBS project which used to show online price tooltip.
*/
function showOnlinePriceOverlayRollover(e) {

WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER').wmBubble('update',WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER').html());
WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER').wmBubble('show');
}
var isRolloverShown = false;
var rolloverIndex = 0;
function showPreferredStoreRollover(e, ind) {
var slapStoresData = WALMART.bot.stores;
var spulStoresData = WALMART.spul.stores;
var storesData = (typeof slapStoresData !== 'undefined' &amp;&amp; slapStoresData &amp;&amp; slapStoresData != '' &amp;&amp; slapStoresData.stores != '') ?
slapStoresData : spulStoresData;
if (storesData != null &amp;&amp; storesData.stores != null &amp;&amp; storesData.stores != '' &amp;&amp; (!isRolloverShown || rolloverIndex != ind)) {
rolloverIndex = ind;
isRolloverShown = true;
setHideTimer(MIN_DISPLAY_TIME);
e = (e) ? e : ((window.event) ? window.event : "")
var el = e.target;
var storeIndex = ind - 1;
resetRollover();
if(storesData.stores[storeIndex]!= undefined &amp;&amp; storesData.stores[storeIndex].address != undefined ){
WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER_CITY').show();
WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER_ADDR1').show();
WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER_ADDR2').show();
WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER_CITY').html( storesData.stores[storeIndex].address.city);
WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER_ADDR1').html(storesData.stores[storeIndex].address.fullStreet);
WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER_ADDR2').html(storesData.stores[storeIndex].address.city + ", " + storesData.stores[storeIndex].address.stateCode + " " + storesData.stores[storeIndex].address.zipCode);
WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER').wmBubble('position',{top:findPosY(el) - 66,left:findPosX(el)});
WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER').wmBubble('update',WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER').html());
WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER').wmBubble('show');
}
}
}

function showSOIRollover(e, desc) {
showRollover(e, desc);
}
function hideRollover(e) {
WALMART.$('#ROLLOVER').wmBubble('hide');
isRolloverShown = false;
clearTimeout(hideTimer);
}
function resetRollover() {
WALMART.$("#ROLLOVER_CITY").hide();
WALMART.$("#ROLLOVER_ADDR1").hide();
WALMART.$("#ROLLOVER_ADDR2").hide();
WALMART.$("#ROLLOVER_OTHER_TEXT").hide();
WALMART.$("#ROLLOVER_CLOSE").hide();
WALMART.$("#ROLLOVER_PICKUP_HOUR").hide();
}
var hideTimer;
function setHideTimer(elapseVal) {
clearTimeout(hideTimer);
hideTimer = setTimeout("hideRollover()", elapseVal);
}
var isOpera = (navigator.userAgent.indexOf('Opera') != -1);
var isIE = (!isOpera &amp;&amp; navigator.userAgent.indexOf('MSIE') != -1)
function getX(e) {
var posx;
if (e.pageX) {
posx = e.pageX;
}
else if (e.clientX) {
posx = e.clientX;
if (isIE) {
posx += top.document.documentElement.scrollLeft + top.document.body.scrollLeft;
}
}
return posx;
}
function getY(e, offset) {
var defaultOffset = 66;
var posy;
if (e.pageY) {
posy = e.pageY;
}
else if (e.clientY) {
posy = e.clientY;
if (isIE) {
posy += top.document.documentElement.scrollTop + top.document.body.scrollTop;
}
}
if (offset == undefined) {
posy -= defaultOffset;
}
else {
posy -= offset
}
return posy;
}

var _getOverlayUrl = function (input) {
var url = '/storeLocator/storeFinderNew.do?serviceName=ALL&amp;sfatt=ALL';
if (typeof input != "undefined" &amp;&amp; input != null) {
url += '&amp;sfsearch_single_line_address=' + escape(input) + '&amp;sfradius=50';
} else if (WALMART.storeFinder.overlay.isPreferredStoreSetInCookie()) {
url += '&amp;sfsearch_single_line_address=' + WALMART.storeFinder.overlay.getZipCodeFromCookie() + '&amp;sfradius=50';
}
return url;
};
function openStoreFinderOverlay(input) {
WALMART.storeFinder.overlay.open(input, 'Select Your Store', _getOverlayUrl);
}

// Start add Omniture R11.8
function url( name )
{
name = name.replace(/[\[]/,"\\\[").replace(/[\]]/,"\\\]");
var regexS = "[\\?&amp;]"+name+"=([^&amp;#]*)";
var regex = new RegExp( regexS );
var results = regex.exec( window.location.href );
if( results == null )
return "";
else
return results[1];
}
// End add Omniture R11.8
function resetSmartSearchVars() {
s_omni.c_w('evar2', null, 0);
s_omni.c_w('evar15', null, 0);
s_omni.c_w('evar26', null, 0);
s_omni.c_w('evar32', null, 0);
s_omni.c_w('evar34', null, 0);
s_omni.c_w('evar35', null, 0);
s_omni.c_w('evar46', null, 0);
s_omni.c_w('evar47', null, 0);
s_omni.c_w('prop8', null, 0);
s_omni.c_w('prop36', '', 0);
s_omni.c_w('event47', null, 0);
s_omni.c_w('event48', null, 0);
s_omni.c_w('evar15', null, 0);
s_omni.c_w('evar16', null, 0);
}
